### 立法院初始化 ###
	## CHI_selected_national_convention - 是否选择国民大会
CHI_legislative_yuan_initial = {
	# 1 - KMT - 国民党 - 654
	# 2 - CPC - 共产党 - 0
	# 3 - CDL - 民盟 - 56
	# 4 - YCP - 青年党 - 10
	# 5 - CDSP - 民社党 - 17
	# 6 - NILL - 独立 - 22
	## 席位总数 ##
	set_variable = {
		CHI_total_legyuan_seat = 759
	}
	set_variable = {
		KMT_party_id = 1
	}
	set_variable = {
		CPC_party_id = 2
	}
	set_variable = {
		CDL_party_id = 3
	}
	set_variable = {
		YCP_party_id = 4
	}
	set_variable = {
		CDSP_party_id = 5
	}
	set_variable = {
		NILL_party_id = 6
	}
	clear_array = CHI_parliament_main_array # 座位数组
	clear_array = CHI_parliament_party_array # 党派数组
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = CHI_selected_national_convention
		}
		clr_country_flag = CHI_selected_national_convention
	}
	## 将State作为结构体载体放到数组中
	# KMT
	add_to_array = {
		CHI_parliament_party_array = 1
	}
	# CPC
	add_to_array = {
		CHI_parliament_party_array = 2
	}
	# CDL
	add_to_array = {
		CHI_parliament_party_array = 3
	}
	# YCP
	add_to_array = {
		CHI_parliament_party_array = 4
	}
	# CDSP
	add_to_array = {
		CHI_parliament_party_array = 5
	}
	# NILL
	add_to_array = {
		CHI_parliament_party_array = 6
	}
	## 党派概览(左面板) ##
	# Flag 汇总
	# CHI_IN_GOVERNMENT - 执政党
	# CHI_BANNED_PARTY - 禁止党派
	# THIS_IS_CPC - 共产党
	# CHI_centrist_op - 中间派
	# CHI_right_wing_op - 右翼
	# CDL_member_party - 民盟
	# CDL_right - 民盟右翼
	# CHI_NO_NEED_FOR_PUBLIC_SUPPORT - 无需支持
	# CHI_obsecure_party - 未知党派
	# 将每一个state中放置党派信息
	# KMT
	1 = {
		CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
		set_variable = {
			CHI_party_leader = 1
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_IN_GOVERNMENT
		set_variable = {
			CHI_parliament_party_seat = 654
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT			# 下一次预计胜选席位
			value = 630
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_KMT_PARTY
	}
	# CPC
	2 = {
		CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
		set_variable = {
			CHI_party_leader = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			CHI_parliament_party_seat = 0
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_BANNED_PARTY
		set_state_flag = THIS_IS_CPC
		set_variable = {
			var = CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT			# 中共影响力
			value = 2
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_CPC_PARTY
	}
	# CDL
	3 = {
		CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
		set_variable = {
			CHI_party_leader = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			CHI_parliament_party_seat = 56
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
			value = 27
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_centrist_op
		set_state_flag = CHI_CDL_PARTY
	}
	# YCP
	4 = {
		CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
		set_variable = {
			CHI_party_leader = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			CHI_parliament_party_seat = 10
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
			value = 14
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_right_wing_op
		set_state_flag = CHI_YCP_PARTY
	}
	# CDSP
	5 = {
		CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
		set_variable = {
			CHI_party_leader = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			CHI_parliament_party_seat = 17
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
			value = 20
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_right_wing_op
		set_state_flag = CHI_CDSP_PARTY
	}
	# NILL
	6 = {
		CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
		set_variable = {
			var = INDEPENDENTS_centrists
			value = 16
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = INDEPENDENTS_progressives
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = INDEPENDENTS_conservatives
			value = 5
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_NO_NEED_FOR_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
		CHI_CAL_INDEPENDENTS_FULL_NUMBER = yes
		set_state_flag = CHI_NILL_PARTY
	}
	CHI_handy_do_it_all = yes
	set_country_flag = china_parliament_activated
}

CHI_parliament_reload = {
	add_to_variable = {
		show_CHI_parliament = 1
	}
}

CHI_party_slot_clear = {
	clear_variable = CHI_parliament_party_seat
	clear_variable = CHI_party_leader
	clear_variable = CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
	clr_state_flag = CHI_IN_GOVERNMENT
	clr_state_flag = CHI_BANNED_PARTY
	clr_state_flag = THIS_IS_CPC
	clr_state_flag = CHI_NO_NEED_FOR_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
	clr_state_flag = CHI_KMT_PARTY
	clr_state_flag = CHI_CPC_PARTY
	clr_state_flag = CHI_CDL_PARTY
	clr_state_flag = CHI_YCP_PARTY
	clr_state_flag = CHI_CDSP_PARTY
	clr_state_flag = CHI_NILL_PARTY
}

### 下届立法院席位变动预测 ###
CHI_SUPPORT_EFFECT = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_party_influence_change_tooltip
	hidden_effect = {
		var:TEMP_CHI_PARTY_ID = {
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				MODIFY_CHI_SUPPORT_LEAN = CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
			}
			set_variable = {
				CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT = MODIFY_CHI_SUPPORT_LEAN
			}
		}
	}
}

### 席位变动 ###
CHI_SEAT_CHANGE_EFFECT = {
	#Excludes 1 and 23
	custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_party_seat_change_tooltip
	hidden_effect = {
		var:TEMP_CHI_PARTY_ID = {
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				MODIFY_CHI_PARTY_SEAT = CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
			set_variable = {
				CHI_parliament_party_seat = MODIFY_CHI_PARTY_SEAT
			}
		}
		# CHI_handy_do_it_all = yes was moved out since we need not just 1
	}
}

# 无党籍席位计算
CHI_independents_calc = {
	#######################
	#Neutral Split - 1-5-4#
	#######################
	##########
	#Progressives
	##########
	set_temp_variable = {
		temp15 = CHI_total_legyuan_seat
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = CHI_parliament_party_array
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_variable = CHI_parliament_party_seat
				}
			}
			subtract_from_temp_variable = {
				temp15 = v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		temp15 = 1
	}
	#add 1
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		temp15 = 0.1
	}
	#Multiply
	round_temp_variable = temp15
	set_variable = {
		INDEPENDENTS_progressives = temp15
	}
	##########
	#Conservatives
	##########
	set_temp_variable = {
		temp16 = CHI_total_legyuan_seat
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = CHI_parliament_party_array
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_variable = CHI_parliament_party_seat
				}
			}
			subtract_from_temp_variable = {
				temp16 = v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		temp16 = 1
	}
	#add 1
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		temp16 = 0.4
	}
	#Multiply
	round_temp_variable = temp16
	set_variable = {
		INDEPENDENTS_conservatives = temp16
	}
	##########
	#Centrists
	##########
	set_temp_variable = {
		temp17 = CHI_total_legyuan_seat
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = CHI_parliament_party_array
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_variable = CHI_parliament_party_seat
				}
			}
			subtract_from_temp_variable = {
				temp17 = v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		temp17 = INDEPENDENTS_conservatives
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		temp17 = INDEPENDENTS_progressives
	}
	set_variable = {
		temp17 = INDEPENDENTS_centrists
	}
}

### 立法院选举 ###
CHI_legislative_yuan_election = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = CHI_parliament_party_array
		# if = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_variable = CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
		# 		# NOT = {
		# 		# 	state = 1
		# 		# }
		# 		NOT = {
		# 			state = 6
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
		set_variable = {
			v:CHI_parliament_party_seat = v:CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
		}
	}
	CHI_independents_calc = yes
	CHI_handy_do_it_all = yes
}

### 立法院简单多数席位计算 ###
CHI_CAL_MAJORITY_NUMBER = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		temp1 = CHI_total_legyuan_seat
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		temp1 = 1
	}
	divide_temp_variable = {
		temp1 = 2
	}
	round_temp_variable = temp1
	set_variable = {
		LEGYUAN_MAJORITY_COUNT = temp1
	}
}

### 立法院绝对多数席位计算 ###
CHI_CAL_SUPER_MAJORITY_NUMBER = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		temp2 = CHI_total_legyuan_seat
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		temp2 = 1
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		temp2 = 2
	}
	divide_temp_variable = {
		temp2 = 3
	}
	round_temp_variable = temp2
	set_variable = {
		LEGYUAN_SUPERMAJORITY_COUNT = temp2
	}
}

### 重新加载议会 ###
reload_CHI_parliament_gui = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		CHI_temp_total = 0
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		selected_party_temp_v = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_of = {
				array = CHI_parliament_party_array
				value = selected_party_temp_v
				var:selected_party_temp_v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_KMT_PARTY
				}
			}
		}
		log = "KMT Seat"
		add_to_temp_array = {
			temp_party = 1
		}
		1 = {
			set_variable = {
				CHI_parliament_party_seat_temp = selected_party_temp_v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_of = {
				array = CHI_parliament_party_array
				value = selected_party_temp_v
				var:selected_party_temp_v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_CPC_PARTY
				}
			}
		}
		log = "CPC Seat"
		add_to_temp_array = {
			temp_party = 2
		}
		2 = {
			set_variable = {
				CHI_parliament_party_seat_temp = selected_party_temp_v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_of = {
				array = CHI_parliament_party_array
				value = selected_party_temp_v
				var:selected_party_temp_v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_CDL_PARTY
				}
			}
		}
		log = "CDL Seat"
		add_to_temp_array = {
			temp_party = 3
		}
		3 = {
			set_variable = {
				CHI_parliament_party_seat_temp = selected_party_temp_v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_of = {
				array = CHI_parliament_party_array
				value = selected_party_temp_v
				var:selected_party_temp_v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_YCP_PARTY
				}
			}
		}
		log = "YCP Seat"
		add_to_temp_array = {
			temp_party = 4
		}
		4 = {
			set_variable = {
				CHI_parliament_party_seat_temp = selected_party_temp_v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_of = {
				array = CHI_parliament_party_array
				value = selected_party_temp_v
				var:selected_party_temp_v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_CDSP_PARTY
				}
			}
		}
		log = "CDSP Seat"
		add_to_temp_array = {
			temp_party = 5
		}
		5 = {
			set_variable = {
				CHI_parliament_party_seat_temp = selected_party_temp_v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_of = {
				array = CHI_parliament_party_array
				value = selected_party_temp_v
				var:selected_party_temp_v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_NILL_PARTY
				}
			}
		}
		log = "NILL Seat"
		add_to_temp_array = {
			temp_party = 6
		}
		6 = {
			set_variable = {
				CHI_parliament_party_seat_temp = selected_party_temp_v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
			}
		}
	}
	# total seat looped
	for_each_loop = {
		array = temp_party
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			CHI_temp_total = v:CHI_parliament_party_seat_temp
		}
		# log = "[?CHI_temp_total]"
		resize_array = {
			array = CHI_parliament_main_array
			value = v
			size = CHI_temp_total
		}
	}
}

CHI_CAL_INDEPENDENTS_FULL_NUMBER = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		temp1 = INDEPENDENTS_centrists
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		temp2 = INDEPENDENTS_progressives
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		temp3 = INDEPENDENTS_conservatives
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		temp1 = temp2
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		temp1 = temp3
	}
	set_variable = {
		INDEPENDENT_total_seat_count = temp1
	}
	set_variable = {
		CHI_parliament_party_seat = INDEPENDENT_total_seat_count
	}
}

CHI_handy_do_it_all = {
	hidden_effect = {
		CHI_sort_party_order = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = CHI_parliament_party_array
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:v = {
						has_state_flag = CHI_NILL_PARTY
					}
				}
				var:v = {
					CHI_CAL_INDEPENDENTS_FULL_NUMBER = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# CHI_SUPPORT_CLAMP = yes
	CHI_CAL_MAJORITY_NUMBER = yes
	CHI_CAL_SUPER_MAJORITY_NUMBER = yes
	CHI_parliament_reload = yes
	reload_CHI_parliament_gui = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = CHI_selected_national_convention
		}
		CHI_national_convention_draw_semicircle = yes
	}
	else = {
		CHI_legislative_yuan_draw_semicircle = yes
	}
}

CHI_sort_party_order = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = CHI_parliament_party_array
		index = i
		# 将纯席位数提取到数组
		add_to_temp_array = {
			seat_of_party_temp_array = v:CHI_parliament_party_seat
		}
		# 创建临时党派数组
		add_to_temp_array = {
			CHI_parliament_party_temp_array = 101
		}
		add_to_temp_array = {
			CHI_parliament_party_temp_array = 102
		}
		add_to_temp_array = {
			CHI_parliament_party_temp_array = 103
		}
		add_to_temp_array = {
			CHI_parliament_party_temp_array = 104
		}
		add_to_temp_array = {
			CHI_parliament_party_temp_array = 105
		}
		add_to_temp_array = {
			CHI_parliament_party_temp_array = 106
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			temp_party = v
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			index_in_temp = 101
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			index_in_temp = i
		}
		log = "SortPartyResult:[?index_in_temp]"
		# 复制一份给临时的，注意后面手动清除state
		var:index_in_temp = {
			CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
			CHI_copy_party = yes
		}
	}
	# temp_array里的也是temp_variable，将无党派设为最小
	set_temp_variable = {
		seat_of_party_temp_array^5 = -1
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		max_party_index = 0
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		max_party_var = 0
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		id = 0
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		# 在临时党派数组里循环
		start = 1
		value = i
		end = 6
		# 查找纯席位数的最大值
		find_highest_in_array = {
			array = seat_of_party_temp_array
			index = max_party_index
		}
		# 按顺序将党派数组依次清零并且放进需要的东西
		var:i = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				max_party_var = CHI_parliament_party_temp_array^max_party_index
			}
			# log = "i:[?i]"
			# log = "S:[?max_party_var:CHI_parliament_party_seat]"
			CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
			# log = "YS:[?max_party_var:CHI_parliament_party_seat]"
			set_temp_variable = {
				temp_party = max_party_var
			}
			CHI_copy_party = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			seat_of_party_temp_array^max_party_index = -1
		}
	}
	# 更新党派id标识
	for_each_loop = {
		array = CHI_parliament_party_array
		index = i
		set_temp_variable = {
			idt = 1
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			i_in_temp = 101
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			idt = i
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			i_in_temp = i
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_KMT_PARTY
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				KMT_party_id = idt
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_CPC_PARTY
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				CPC_party_id = idt
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_CDL_PARTY
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				CDL_party_id = idt
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_YCP_PARTY
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				YCP_party_id = idt
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_CDSP_PARTY
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				CDSP_party_id = idt
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:v = {
					has_state_flag = CHI_NILL_PARTY
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				NILL_party_id = idt
			}
		}
		# 清除临时state
		var:i_in_temp = {
			CHI_party_slot_clear = yes
		}
	}
}

CHI_copy_party = {
	set_variable = {
		CHI_parliament_party_seat = temp_party:CHI_parliament_party_seat
	}
	set_variable = {
		CHI_party_leader = temp_party:CHI_party_leader
	}
	set_variable = {
		CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT = temp_party:CHI_PARTY_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_IN_GOVERNMENT
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_IN_GOVERNMENT
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_BANNED_PARTY
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_BANNED_PARTY
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = THIS_IS_CPC
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = THIS_IS_CPC
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_NO_NEED_FOR_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_NO_NEED_FOR_PUBLIC_SUPPORT
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_KMT_PARTY
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_KMT_PARTY
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_CPC_PARTY
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_CPC_PARTY
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_CDL_PARTY
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_CDL_PARTY
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_YCP_PARTY
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_YCP_PARTY
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_CDSP_PARTY
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_CDSP_PARTY
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:temp_party = {
				has_state_flag = CHI_NILL_PARTY
			}
		}
		set_state_flag = CHI_NILL_PARTY
	}
}

CHI_disable_legislative_yuan = {
	clear_variable = CHI_total_legyuan_seat
	clear_array = CHI_parliament_party_array
	clear_array = CHI_parliament_main_array
	CHI_handy_do_it_all = yes
}

CHI_dissolve_party_in_legislative_yuan = {
	var:TEMP_CHI_PARTY_ID = {
		set_state_flag = CHI_BANNED_PARTY
	}
	CHI_handy_do_it_all = yes
}

CHI_undissolve_party_in_legislative_yuan = {
	var:TEMP_CHI_PARTY_ID = {
		clr_state_flag = CHI_BANNED_PARTY
	}
	CHI_handy_do_it_all = yes
}
